<tr>
<th>Extra Information
</th>
<td>Two editions (different engravings) were issued in the composer's lifetime by Durand. The first edition was published in November 1891, the second in 1904. The plate numbers (4395, 4396) were retained for the 1904 edition, even though it is an entirely new engraving.
</td></tr></table>
